Hygiene: The hotel's facilities are very old, the window glass is dirty, the wallpaper in the bathroom is mottled, the room has a strong musty smell, and the carpet has a faint smell.

Service: The little brother who checked in was kind and friendly, but the staff I encountered at other times were quite indifferent.

Environment: It is quite convenient to go anywhere by car.

The shower hardware in the bathroom is all too low, which is no different from ordinary budget hotels. After entering the room and discharging the card, only the TV screen is on, and no other lights are on. They are all brainless designs. The pressure is also very low, and the water is quite gentle.
